<gmap_id>0x54d2ed1718927b3f:0x51aa5b412706141a<//gmap_id><rating>5</rating>< Text>
The diesel horse Bridge construction was started on 1914 and is one of the oldest Bridges intended for cars .
this bridge has been in service
for a very long time.
Now it's part of the Sacramento River Trail for bicyclists skateboarders and Walkers alike.
this bridge was retired in 1997 with a modern bridge.
but this Old Bridge was kept on the side as part of the historic landmarks in the area.
So if you want to go cruise around on the Sacramento River Trail take in the sites that Redding has to offer and see a little bit of History.
check out the diesel horse Bridge.<//Text>

<Time>1500948182055< /Time><Rate>1< /Rate><text>Completely dishonest company who preys on stranded motorists by using deceptive scare tactics and false claims

My car was overheating about 20 miles outside of Baker and roadside service sent out Ken's towing.

A guy named David showed up and in less than 30 seconds, I had already caught him in his first of many lies.

He tried to manipulate, cheat and lie his way to convince me to pay $550 for a tow, even though I insisted that the vehicle just needed coolant which he didn't have. When I called roadside assistance, I specifically asked them to have the driver bring coolant, a message that David claimed to never receive.

In less than 2 minutes, in the dark, David was able to diagnose my vehicles as having a blown head gasket, and explained that I had no other alternative than to tow it. He gave me a list of completely bogus reasons why he knew the head gasket was blown. He must have just assumed that I was some dumb motorist with no basic knowledge of cars who he could easily take advantage of. He clearly didn't realize that I have worked at a car dealership for the past 12 years.

I persisted that I believed the vehicle just needed coolant and and he continued to come up with false arguments for his cause.

He lied repeatedly and used manipulation, threats, guilt and scare tactics to try to get me to agree to let him tow.

At first, he wouldn't even tell me a price to be towed. I had to ask him three separate times before he actually asked me how much I was willing to pay? Don't most tow companies either have a flat rate or charge by the mile?

Finally he blurted out $550.  I told him politely that I was not going to pay 550 for him to tow me and that I was going to call people in Vegas and that his services were no longer needed.

When he finally realized that I wasn't going to submit to his misleading tactics, he suddenly remembered that he had water on his truck that we could fill the radiator with. Amazing that this hadn't been an option for the last 30 minutes.

He agreed to fill me up with water for the price of $110, and he told me that "when you break down again, I'm not going to come save you".

After I left David, I drove 460 miles straight at 70 mph with my a/c on full blast and I never had another problem the rest of the way. In fact, the temperature gauge didn't get past the halfway point the entire rest of my trip. Not too shabby for having a blown head gasket.

I assume that most people he encounters just fall for his scam and his dishonesty, but I wasn't about to. It got to be so bad that even my wife realized what he was trying to do and started video and audio recording him.

I will be filing complaints with the roadside service company that I called as well as the state and the better business bureau.

I believe that all businesses need to make money and they need to be paid for their services, but I don't believe that any business should ever take advantage of stranded motorists by deceiving them with false claims in an attempt to trick them into gouging for services that they don't need. Shame on David and shame on Ken's towing.</text>< Pictures>

<rating>5< /rating>< text>
Of the many vets I have worked with, Dr. Hazanow ranks at the very top. She helped us care for Aidan, our Irish Setter dog, in his elder years. He enjoyed a long life for his breed, but the last couple of years was tough, as he developed bladder disease and complications. Dr. Hazanow provided empathic problem-solving care that was clinically competent and highly attuned to both Aidan's needs and our needs as his caregivers. Never were we rushed through an appointment. Charges are reasonable and I never felt that anything being recommended--procedures, medications, or other care products--had any taint of profit motive. Indeed, Dr. Hazanow several times suggested cost-effective solutions available from the drugstore or the supermarket. When she was not available, Drs. Knobel and Whitaker could also be relied on to provide excellent patient and family centered care, and the support staff were competent and very helpful. A couple minor front desk problems I experienced could have happened anywhere and the staff were apologetic and quick to fix them. Seven Hills is a veterinary practice and facility where you and your family can expect high quality, respectful client-centered services and supports for your pet.< /text>

<Text>Authentically delicious !
I have been meaning to do this review for some time now.  I discovered this little place over a year ago, while in the area.

This place is nice and clean and you may eat on the patio, take out or eat inside.
I have had several items on the menu and never been let down.
Leno is the owner and He really knows what he's doing.

I love the consistency of flavors, never wavering!  My favorites are his Chili Colorado, the meat nearly melts in your mouth it is so tender!
The Chili Verde is wonderful sometimes a tad bit spicy, but never overpowering.
If you just want the best beans and rice in town well this is it!

So not only is the price right, but the food is very good!
Thank you for great food and great service!
Way to go Leno!

< Text>
Of all the tacos I've ever had, this place was, and I don't say this lightly, THE BEST! Leno was there when I came in. I heard the meat is a little different when he's there (not sure if that's true). The menu had a nice variety but I had to get tacos. So I got chicharron, shrimp, and carnitas tacos. AMAZING! The meats and shrimp were perfectly cooked, wonderful flavor. They toast up the corn tortilla a bit so that added a nice dimension of flavor and texture I enjoyed. And the green salsa was legit. I was surprised they had melon juice and thats my favorite so I ordered theirs. It was a nice accompaniment to the INSANE tacos. I love this place and I look forward to eating here again.<//Text>
